It unzips multiple files simultaneously up to the limit of your CPU, memory, and disk drive performance to unzip files as quickly as possible. \r\n\r\nThere are now 2 ways to unzip files using this app:\r\n1.\tUnzip all files into the same directories as the zip files.\r\n        a.\tClick the Zip Files Folder Path Browse button and select a folder with one or more Zip files in it. \r\n        b.\tClick the Go button.\r\n        c.\tAll zip files in that folder and in any sub-folders of that folder will be unzipped in place. \r\n\r\n2.\tUnzip the files to an output folder.\r\n        a.\tClick the Zip Files Folder Path Browse button and select a folder with one or more Zip files in it. \r\n        b.\tClick the Output Folder Path Browse button and select the output folder.\r\n        c.\tClick the Go button.\r\n        d.\tAll zip files in that folder and in any sub-folders of that folder will be unzipped to the specified Output Folder.
